# <a name="call-built-in-excel-worksheet-functions"></a><span data-ttu-id="72a3c-102">???? Excel ?????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-102">Call built-in Excel worksheet functions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="72a3c-103">????????? Excel JavaScript API ???? Excel ??????? `VLOOKUP` ? `SUM`??</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-103">This article explains how to call built-in Excel worksheet functions such as `VLOOKUP` and `SUM` using the Excel JavaScript API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="72a3c-104">?????????? Excel JavaScript API ????? Excel ???????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-104">It also provides the full list of built-in Excel worksheet functions that can be called using the Excel JavaScript API.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="72a3c-105">???????? Excel JavaScript API ? Excel ???*?????*????[? Excel ????????](custom-functions-overview.md)?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-105">For information about how to create *custom functions* in Excel using the Excel JavaScript API, see [Create custom functions in Excel](custom-functions-overview.md).</span></span>

## <a name="calling-a-worksheet-function"></a><span data-ttu-id="72a3c-106">???????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-106">Calling a worksheet function</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="72a3c-107">?????????????????????? `sampleFunction()` ????????????????????????????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-107">The following code snippet shows how to call a worksheet function, where `sampleFunction()` is a placeholder that should be replaced with the name of the function to call and the input parameters that the function requires.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="72a3c-108">???????? **FunctionResult** ??? **value** ????????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-108">The **value** property of the **FunctionResult** object that's returned by a worksheet function contains the result of the specified function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="72a3c-109">??????????? **FunctionResult** ??? **value** ???? `load` ???????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-109">As this example shows, you must `load` the **value** property of the **FunctionResult** object before you can read it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="72a3c-110">???????????????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-110">In this example, the result of the function is simply being written to the console.</span></span> 

```js
var functionResult = context.workbook.functions.sampleFunction(); 
functionResult.load('value');
return context.sync()
    .then(function () {
        console.log('Result of the function: ' + functionResult.value);
    });
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="72a3c-111">?????? Excel JavaScript API ??????????????[????????](#supported-worksheet-functions)???</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-111">See the [Supported worksheet functions](#supported-worksheet-functions) section of this article for a list of functions that can be called using the Excel JavaScript API.</span></span>

## <a name="sample-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="72a3c-112">????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-112">Sample data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="72a3c-113">????? Excel ??????????????????????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-113">The following image shows a table in an Excel worksheet that contains sales data for various types of tools over a three month period.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="72a3c-114">???????????????????????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-114">Each number in the table represents the number of units sold for a specific tool in a specific month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="72a3c-115">????????????????????????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-115">The examples that follow will show how to apply built-in worksheet functions to this data.</span></span>

![????????? 11 ??12 ?? 1 ?????? Excel ????](../images/worksheet-functions-chaining-results.jpg)

## <a name="example-1-single-function"></a><span data-ttu-id="72a3c-117">?? 1????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-117">Example 1: Single function</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="72a3c-118">???????????????? `VLOOKUP` ?????? 11 ????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-118">The following code sample applies the `VLOOKUP` function to the sample data described previously to identify the number of wrenches sold in November.</span></span>

```js
Excel.run(function (context) {
    var range = context.workbook.worksheets.getItem("Sheet1").getRange("A1:D4");
    var unitSoldInNov = context.workbook.functions.vlookup("Wrench", range, 2, false);
    unitSoldInNov.load('value');

    return context.sync()
        .then(function () {
            console.log(' Number of wrenches sold in November = ' + unitSoldInNov.value);
        });
}).catch(errorHandlerFunction);
```

## <a name="example-2-nested-functions"></a><span data-ttu-id="72a3c-119">?? 2?????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-119">Example 2: Nested functions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="72a3c-120">???????????????? `VLOOKUP` ???????? 11 ?? 12 ????????????? `SUM` ??????????????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-120">The following code sample applies the `VLOOKUP` function to the sample data described previously to identify the number of wrenches sold in November and the number of wrenches sold in December, and then applies the `SUM` function to calculate the total number of wrenches sold during those two months.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="72a3c-121">?????????????????????????????????????????????????? `sumOfTwoLookups`??? `load` ?????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-121">As this example shows, when one or more function calls are nested within another function call, you only need to `load` the final result that you subsequently want to read (in this example, `sumOfTwoLookups`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="72a3c-122">????????????????????? `VLOOKUP` ???????????????????????</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="72a3c-122">Any intermediate results (in this example, the result of each `VLOOKUP` function) will be calculated and used to calculate the final result.</span></span>

```js
Excel.run(function (context) {
    var range = context.workbook.worksheets.getItem("Sheet1").getRange("A1:D4");
    var sumOfTwoLookups = context.workbook.functions.sum(
        context.workbook.functions.vlookup("Wrench", range, 2, false), 
        context.workbook.functions.vlookup("Wrench", range, 3, false)
    );
    sumOfTwoLookups.load('value');

    return context.sync()
        .then(function () {
            console.log(' Number of wrenches sold in November and December = ' + sumOfTwoLookups.value);
        });
}).catch(errorHandlerFunction);
```
